 Dr
 chandra rajan kaa maananaa he ki is bill main kaaphi kanfusion he

 ganga dashahra yani maa ganga ke dharti par aane kaa din
 This is the day to fulfill the wishes and get the boon from the mother
 is baar yah parv somvaar, 21 june 2010 ko manaaya ja rahaa he
 On this occasion, a dip in the fallen Ganges can change your luck
 is baar chitra nakshatra somvaar ko padane kii vajah se ganga dashahra par aapako mil saktaa he das guna adhik fal
 For this auspicious occasion, some special things are mentioned below, which can relieve you of the troubles of your life
 New Morning: • Take 10 dips in the Ganges in the morning
 • ghar main hon to pani main gangaajal daalkar 10 lote jal daalen
 • Give the mean of the sun
 • makarvahini ganga kaa chitra rakhkar puja karen
 • Offer 10 types of flowers, fruits, sweets in worship
 • dhoop, deep, navaidya arpit karen
 • Hoon and Shri Shrin Bhagwati Gange Namo Namah: Chant a garland of mantras
 • 10 brahmanon ko vastra daan karen
 • Plant Lakshmi Peepal tree
 aisa karne se sukh-saubhaahgya ghar main bad jayega or dhan kii varsha hogi
 What to do for job advancement: • 5 AM to 9 AM
 55 baje ke bich ganga main snaan karen
 • Take 10 dips facing east
 • surya ko ardhya den
 • Salute the elders
 • shiv shakti kii aradhana karen
 • Offer water, sandalwood, belpatra, durva and naivedya on Shiva
 • uun gan siddhidatri ganga devyai nam: mantra ke ek maala kaa jaap kare
 • Feed sweets to 10 girls
 • jamun kaa ped lagaaein

 • dhoop, deep, naivedhy, se aarti karen
 • Recite Lakshmi, Stuti, or Ganesh Stroth
 • uun makar vahinyai lakshmi sah bhaaginyai gangaayi nam: mantra ek maala jap karen
 • Donate sixteen fist barley, rice, umbrella with right hand to 10 Brahmins
 • anaar kaa ped lagaaenye upaay karne se aapke sabhi band kaam chaalu ho jaaenge or kaarobaar bhi chamak uthegaa

 • surya ko ardhya den

 • abhishek ke baad itr, vastra, roli, mauli phool durva chadhayen

 • uun kan kameshwarai gangaayi nam: mantra kii ek maala jaap karen
 • Serve the old and poor
 • kadamb kaa ped lagaaein

 • makarvahini ganga kii puja karen

 • Give flour, lentils, sugar, white cloth grains to 10 Brahmins
 • pati-patni main prem badhegaa
 • Family prosperity will increase

 • If you are sick, remember the Ganges
 • gangaajal se aachman karen
 • Sprinkle water on your body twelve times
